The `ClientBrief.industryKnowledge` field is already optional, so absence stays a clean no-op. **(b) `clients.industry` placeholder bug fixed.** `verify-code` seeds `clients.industry` with `'Pending — captured in chat'`. No code was overwriting it — every conversationally-onboarded client carried the placeholder forever. `business-identity` now accepts an optional `industry` param; the conversation shell sends `extraction.industryFreeText` (preserves the customer's own framing for unmapped industries) or the mapped industry's display name. Idempotency check includes industry; empty industry skips the column update so back-compat callers are unaffected. Brand-side reads were always fine — generation reads `brands.industry_category` which the `wizard-assets` path writes. **Drifts deliberately left as documented divergence (NOT fixed):** (i) **voice default** — conversational hardcodes `NEUTRAL_VOICE` (3/3/3) in `derive-brief.ts:264`; concierge uses `VOICE_TONE_PRESETS.friendlyLocal` (2/2/2) in `CreateClientModal.tsx:201`. Same industry, same brand colors, slightly different voice axis flowing into the prompt — acceptable since `friendlyLocal` lives in shared `voice-presets.ts` and either can be retuned without a structural change. (ii) **`audience` axis** — conversational hardcodes `'mixed'`; concierge captures from operator chips. Conservative default, generation tolerates both. (iii) **business-contact field capture asymmetry** — `business.phone` / `ownerName` / `offer` are empty on conversational (deliberately skipped turns) but captured on concierge; the generator's `BusinessDetails` interface tolerates absence. (iv) **Lifecycle bypass** — concierge writes `lifecycle_status='active'` directly (intentional Pattern B design — operator is the verifier; payment collected out-of-band). (v) **Capability grants** — only conversational triggers the 0088 auto-grant on signup; concierge creates no end-user, the first invite-accept triggers the grant. **Trigger to revisit:** if telemetry shows the voice drift produces noticeably different copy quality, standardise to `friendlyLocal` (`derive-brief.ts:264`); if operators report stale `'Pending — captured in chat'` strings in existing clients' filters, ship a one-shot backfill UPDATE migrating those rows to the corresponding `brands.industry_category`.

- **Bundle-aware `<BundleButton>` primitive — RESOLVED in C2b-3; full migration is the follow-up.** `lib/website/sections/_shared/BundleButton.tsx` reads `--bundle-radius-button` / `--bundle-button-style` / `--bundle-shadow-elevation` at render time and renders the correct bundle treatment. Variants: `primary` (filled by default; the `outlined-or-text` bundle reframes as outlined) + `secondary` (outlined by default; reframed as a text link). Built on `SurfaceLink` so editor click-to-select still works. The `big-bold-arrow` bundle (Bold & Direct) promotes the trailing glyph to a permanent `→` when the caller didn't pass one. **Adopted in two reference sections** — `about` (`extra='button'`) and `features` (bottom CTA). The remaining 7 customer-facing CTA sections (hero / offer / gallery / reviews / contact / cta / faq) still render inline-styled `SurfaceLink` chains; migrating them is the follow-up — kept out of C2b-3 so visual regressions stay contained to the sections that PR is already changing. Pattern for the follow-up: swap each section's inline `<SurfaceLink className="inline-flex items-center rounded-lg px-6 py-3 …">` for `<BundleButton variant={style === 'outline' ? 'secondary' : 'primary'} accent={accent}>{label}</BundleButton>`. Verify the editor preview + the live render for each bundle (radius / weight / hover shadow / outlined-or-text reframing). The `cta` section's dual-CTA path needs both primary + secondary; the `header` / `footer` CTAs may or may not migrate (operator brand-mark area — call when the migration session lands).

- **Services section deprecation — RESOLVED in C2b-3.** `services` (the deprecated section type — distinct from `'services'` the PageType, which is the URL slug for a services landing page and stays as it is) is removed from the GENERATION path: (1) `isEligible` in `generation-prompt.ts` drops `implemented: false` sections from the model-facing catalog so the prompt no longer offers `services` as a placement target; (2) `coerceDeprecatedSection` in `generation-validation.ts` runs as Pass A0 in both website + funnel pipelines — a stray `services` section the model still emits gets coerced into a `features` section, lifting `services[]` rows into `items[]` with price + duration folded onto the description so no captured data is lost. Logged via `generation_log` as `reason='invalid'` / `fieldName='__sectionType'` for telemetry. **The `services.tsx` file STAYS** — `data-stub.tsx` (website + funnel) still renders pre-existing seed pages built against the section, and `sections/index.ts` still registers `servicesSection` so the editor renders them. Deleting the file would orphan the Voltline + FreshHome seed pages. **The future deletion path** (when seed data is also migrated): convert each `mkSection('…', 'services', …)` call in both `data-stub.tsx` files to `mkSection('…', 'features', …)` using the same shape `coerceDeprecatedSection`'s `map` function produces, then delete `services.tsx` + remove the `servicesSection` import + remove `servicesMeta` from `SECTION_REGISTRY_META`. Run the editor and confirm the converted seed pages render correctly before deletion.

- **Trust V3 single-word labels — RESOLVED in C2b-3.** `display='compact-icons'` (the thin horizontal band) renders each item as `icon + label` and assumes single-word labels ("Insured", "Vetted", "Local"). The model frequently emits multi-word phrases that break the rhythm. **Enforcement:** `enforceTrustCompactSingleWord` in `generation-validation.ts` runs as Pass B++ in both pipelines (after enum validation + bundle variant assignment, so a bundle promotion to `compact-icons` triggers it too) — multi-word labels get abbreviated to the first word, trailing punctuation stripped. "Insured & bonded" → "Insured". The `SECTION_SHAPE_CATALOG` `display` guidance was also hardened with explicit examples + a note that single-word is required + the pipeline enforces. Logged per-item as `reason='invalid'` so `generation_log` telemetry surfaces which industries' label vocabulary collides with the V3 layout.

- **Item-array asymmetry primitive (`featuredIndex`) — wired in `features` for V1 in C2b-3, pattern documented for V1.1 reuse.** `FeaturesData.featuredIndex: number | null` — when set on the cards layout, the indexed item renders as a wider (2-column-span) card with larger typography. `null` = uniform grid (the pre-C2b-3 behaviour). Editor surface: a `Featured item` picker on the items element-inspector, using `'none' | 'idx-N'` string sentinels because `VariantField` only takes string ids. **The pattern is documented in the FeaturesData doc comment** with explicit reuse guidance for V1.1 expansion to services / reviews / trust / faq / gallery / offer — same field shape, same editor pattern, same Preview clamp + grid-span branch. NOT exposed to the AI by default (the brief usually wants a uniform grid; over-suggesting causes the model to always set it); operators surface it editorially.

- **About V2 story-arc + Features V1/V3 layout variants — RESOLVED in C2b-3.** Two new sets of section variants land via the bundle steering layer. **About**: `layout: 'split' | 'story-arc'` — `split` (default) keeps the existing 2-column copy+media layout (V1 text+photo, V3 stats-brief via `extra='stats'`); `story-arc` (V2) is the new vertical narrative — eyebrow + headline + lead paragraph (the existing `sub` field) + 2-3 chapters (the new `chapters[]`) + optional middle pull-quote (the new `pullQuote`) + optional bottom team photo (the existing `imageUrl`). Single column, max-w-[720px] for line-length readability. Split-layout fields hide in the editor when story-arc is active. **Features**: `layout: 'cards' | 'plain' | 'numbered' | 'dark-band'` — `cards` (default) is V2 icon grid; `numbered` (V1) is a vertical stack with big bold numbers as the visual element (no icons / images); `dark-band` (V3) is a full-bleed dark surface tinted by `--palette-surface-3` with a horizontal row at `@2xl` that stacks vertically below the breakpoint. The `FeaturesItems` sub-component dispatches on layout so each variant's surface is straightforward to extend on its own. **Bundle steering**: variantRules narrow the layout pick per bundle (see `design-bundles.ts`). `sharp_direct` → about=split, features=numbered|dark-band. `warm_established` → about=split|story-arc, features=cards. `clean_premium` → about=story-arc, features=cards|dark-band. `bold_direct` → about=split + extra=stats (the V3 stats-brief register), features=numbered|cards|dark-band. The `bold_direct` rule narrows TWO keys (`layout` + `extra`) — `assignBundleVariants` already iterates `Object.keys(rule)`, so the dual-key shape works without any pipeline change.

- **C3 V1 funnel polish — RESOLVED (seven fixes A / C / D / E / F / G / H; FIX B deferred to V1.1).** The C3 V1 PR shipped the integrity + polish fixes the funnel audit surfaced; the trust-signal preflight rule (FIX B) was deferred as a separate parked decision below.
  - **FIX A — Phone + address capture at step 2.** `/api/forms/submit`'s existing-lead branch now reads phone + address from the qualification form's tagged fields and COALESCE-updates `customers.phone` / `customers.address` and `leads.customer_phone_snapshot`. First-non-null wins so an operator-edited customer value is never clobbered by a stale follow-up submission. Required adding `'address'` to `FormFieldLeadRole` (`form-config.ts`) + tagging the qualification form's address field in `buildQualificationFormConfig` (`generate-funnel-live.ts`). Previously step-2-completed leads showed no phone in the operator inbox because phone landed in `lead_events.payload` only — verifiable on production data by checking `customers.phone IS NULL AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM lead_events WHERE lead_id = leads.id AND kind = 'form_submitted' AND payload->>'fields' ILIKE '%phone%')`. **Trigger to revisit:** if a new customer attribute needs propagating (e.g. preferred-contact-method, marketing consent), add it to `FormFieldLeadRole` AND extract it in the existing-lead branch's `fieldRole` helper — never via field-name regex / heuristic.
  - **FIX C — FAQ section added between trust and reviews #2 in funnel step 1.** Step-1 grows from 7 to 8 sections: `hero → offer → reviews → features → trust → faq → reviews → form`. The FAQ section is a real objection-handler — `LEAD_CAPTURE_SECTION_PLAN` brief tells the model to lean on the Industry context block's "Common customer objections and how to handle them in copy" list (the `objectionHandlers` array on `industry-templates.ts` — already emitted by `renderIndustryPromptBlock` so no new prompt block was needed). 4–6 Q&As, each question phrased in the customer's own words, each answer 1–2 specific sentences. The worked example carries four FAQs that paraphrase the electrician template's three objectionHandlers + adds one (the bill-before-work answer) so the model sees the pattern. The validation pipeline's `expectedTypes` was extended and the "EXACTLY seven sections" rule became "EXACTLY eight". **The Suby/Sultanic locked architecture is preserved** — every other section's role + the canonical order is unchanged; FAQ is an insertion, not a rewrite. **Trigger to revisit:** if telemetry shows the FAQ section underperforming (operators consistently delete it post-generation), drop it from `LEAD_CAPTURE_SECTION_PLAN` + reduce `expectedTypes` to 7 — the rest of the prompt is FAQ-agnostic.
  - **FIX D — Per-funnel guard on existingLeadId tightened.** Covered in the "Funnel lead threading uses ?lead=" entry above — the existing-lead select now reads `source_funnel_id`, mismatched funnel ids reject as the same generic 400, NULL `source_funnel_id` heals forward on the current request. Closes the gap where a website lead could be appended to from any funnel via a guessed leadId.
  - **FIX E — funnelId threaded through editor test-submit.** Covered in the analytics block above (under "Editor test-submit attribution — RESOLVED"). `FormTestSubmitContext` + `CreateLeadInput` gained an optional `funnelId`; `SectionEditor` passes `mode.funnel.id` when the editor mode is `funnelStep`; `submitLead` writes `source_funnel_id` on funnel test-submits.
  - **FIX F — Step indicator on multi-step funnels.** `lib/public-site/resolve.ts`'s funnel target surface gained `stepIndex` (0-based) + `stepCount`. The resolver was already computing `idx` for `nextStepHref`; the addition is a single line. `PublicSiteRenderer`'s funnel branch mounts a new `<FunnelStepIndicator>` (`src/components/public-site/FunnelStepIndicator.tsx`) above `<main>`. The component self-gates — returns null when `stepCount <= 1` (single-step funnel) OR `stepIndex <= 0` (the landing). The landing step deliberately has no indicator because the first visitor impression doesn't benefit from "you're 1/N here"; the indicator helps once they've committed to a second step. Styling is intentionally minimal — a mono `Step N of M` label + a brand-accent progress bar reading inclusive percentage (step 2 of 3 = 67%). The fill colour reads `brand.accentColor` so the indicator matches the funnel's design bundle. Mobile-stacks via `flex-col sm:flex-row`. **Trigger to revisit:** if a 4+ step funnel ships (today's funnels are landing → schedule → thanks), the same component already handles the math.
  - **FIX G — `data-stub.tsx` deprecated section references cleaned.** Voltline's seed funnel previously used the deprecated `services` section type on the landing step + the deprecated `schedulePicker` section type as the entire schedule step. Both have been swapped to current shapes: `services` → `features` (the value-stack equivalent the live generator emits), `schedulePicker` → a `form` section with a `Section.form` envelope carrying a qualification FormConfig (phone + address + date + time-of-day + budget — same shape as `buildQualificationFormConfig`). `mkSection` gained an optional `form` arg for the envelope attach. The seed is reached only by the `voltlinePassthrough` no-brief fallback in `generation-stub.ts` (a back-compat path); this cleanup means a fresh reader of the codebase doesn't trip over deprecated section types in seed data.
  - **FIX H — `schedulePicker` marked deprecated in registry-meta.** Flipped to `implemented: false` (matches the `services` precedent — `servicesMeta` also carries `implemented: false`). `AddSectionDialog` filters on `implemented: true` so the picker no longer offers the type. The section file (`sections/schedulePicker.tsx`) + the `sections/index.ts` registration + the `section_type` DB enum value all STAY — a legacy `funnel_versions.snapshot` row could still reference the type, and removing the registration would break that render. **Plan: remove `schedulePicker.tsx` + its `sections/index.ts` line once no `funnel_versions.snapshot` in production references this type** (verifiable by `SELECT count(*) FROM funnel_versions, jsonb_array_elements(snapshot->'steps') step, jsonb_array_elements(step->'sections') section WHERE section->>'type' = 'schedulePicker'`).

- **PARKED — Funnel trust-signal preflight (V1.1) — FIX B was deliberately not built in C3 V1.** The website preflight has a `reviews-ai-placeholder` rule that catches AI-invented testimonials by stashing a `placeholderSnapshot` on the section's `ai` meta at generation time, then exact-matching at preflight time. The funnel pipeline (`generate-funnel-live.ts`) deliberately does NOT write `placeholderSnapshot` today (parked decision: "Funnel-generated reviews are NOT covered" by the placeholder snapshot pattern). A funnel trust-signal preflight rule needs an equivalent ground-truth source — pure-heuristic detection (regex for cert numbers like `EC10437`, specific percentages like `98%`, star ratings, review counts) is too noisy because legitimate operator-supplied trust signals match the same patterns. Three approaches for V1.1: (a) extend the `placeholderSnapshot` shape with a `trust?: PlaceholderTrustSnapshot[]` slot AND make `generate-funnel-live.ts` write the snapshot for trust sections — reverses the funnel generator's "no snapshot" parked decision but is the cleanest pattern; (b) operator manual review during preflight (current state — fabricated trust signals slip through unless the operator catches them); (c) pure heuristic regex with a false-positive rate so high it gets ignored. **Trigger to revisit:** real customer signal that fabricated certifications / percentages are causing credibility issues on live funnels — until then, operator manual review is the V1 mitigation, and trust signals are editable post-publish via the section editor.

- **C3 V1 funnel polish — `FunnelStepIndicator` is the first piece of funnel-level chrome.** Up to C3 V1, the funnel renderer (`PublicSiteRenderer`'s `kind: 'funnel'` branch) wrapped a `<main>` with the funnel's sections and nothing else (no header, no footer, no nav — the design-doc invariant). `FunnelStepIndicator` mounts above `<main>` and is the first piece of funnel-level chrome to land. **Trigger to revisit the chrome boundary:** if a second funnel-level chrome surface lands (e.g. a sticky "Step 1 of 2" header, an exit-intent modal, a trust badge bar that floats), promote the chrome to a `<FunnelChrome>` wrapper component or extend `FunnelStepIndicator` with slots — the current single-component design is fine because there's only one chrome element.

- **Post-conversational-signup visibility race — RESOLVED.** Symptom: a customer clicking "View in editor" the instant `genPhase='ready'` lights up lands on `/website`'s OPERATOR-targeting empty state ("operator can spin one up below") for 10-30s, while React Query's background refetch catches the new `websites` row. Three layered fixes shipped together:
  - **(1) Visibility probe** (`src/lib/onboarding/visibility-probe.ts`). After `runConversationGeneration` returns `ok` (wizard-assets POST committed server-side), the conversation shell holds the blueprint overlay at the existing `'persisting'` stage and polls `fetchWebsiteForClient` + `fetchFunnelsForClient` (the SAME RLS-bound queries `/website` will run on landing) at 1.5s intervals until both return data. Only then does `setGenPhase('ready')` enable the editor CTA. Timeout ceiling = 30s — on timeout we still flip to `ready` with a soft warning ("if the editor screen looks empty for a moment, refresh once") rather than blocking the customer; the row is real and a stale read resolves on the next refetch. Both `fetchWebsiteForClient` and `fetchFunnelsForClient` were promoted from module-private to exported with comments tying them to the probe. **Trigger to revisit:** if a future generation path ships site-only (no funnel), pass `expectFunnel: false` to the probe.
  - **(2) Role-aware `/website` empty state** (`src/app/website/page.tsx`). `NoWebsiteState` now takes `viewerRole`. Operator-role keeps the existing "operator can spin one up below" copy + `ScaffoldWebsiteButton`; client-role gets a tailored "Your site is being built" loading card via the new sibling `ClientGenerationInProgressState`, which auto-polls the website query every 1.5s and self-heals into the real hub when the row lands. After 30s of polling the card flips to a "still finishing — refresh now" affordance with a manual reload button so the customer isn't stuck on the spinner without agency. This handles the refresh-mid-generation case the visibility probe can't reach (the probe lives on the chat surface; once the customer leaves it, only `/website` can recover).
  - **(3) Scaffold gate moved from cap to role.** `ScaffoldWebsiteButton` was previously gated only by `<CapabilityGate capability="editPages">` — clients hold `editPages` via `CLIENT_OWNER_DEFAULTS` so they saw the scaffold CTA, which is wrong (Scaffold is an operator-concierge action; a client should never be offered to spin up a website for "themselves" via this path). The new gate is `viewerRole === 'admin'` AND the cap (defence in depth). Clients in the no-website state see the loading card only — no Scaffold affordance, no operator-targeted copy.
  - **Why three fixes for one report:** the user-visible symptom was the loading race, but the screenshot showed the empty state was ALSO wrong in role-targeting + wrong in offered actions. Shipping only fix (1) would leave a customer-on-refresh seeing the operator empty state; shipping only fix (2)+(3) would leave the happy-path race intact (the chat would still send them to /website with no site visible). All three needed to land together.
